99.1</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white"><IMG SRC="ex99-1_001.jpg" ALT=""></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: center; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>RenovoRx
Reports Second Quarter 2022 Financial Results</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Los
Altos, CA, August 15, 2022</B> - RenovoRx, Inc. (Nasdaq: RNXT), a biopharmaceutical company focused on the localized treatment of difficult-to-treat
solid tumors through its proprietary RenovoRx Trans-Arterial Micro-Perfusion (RenovoTAMP<SUP>TM</SUP>) therapy platform, today reported
its financial results for the quarter ended June 30, 2022.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">&ldquo;Over
the past decade, our team has developed and refined a unique therapy platform for difficult-to-treat solid tumors by localizing and targeting
chemotherapy to minimize systemic side-effects, improve quality of life, and potentially extend life. We started with one of the
most aggressive tumor types - pancreatic cancer,&rdquo; said Shaun Bagai, CEO of RenovoRx. &ldquo;Innovation and success in treatment
options for pancreatic cancer are sparse. Through our Phase 3 TIGeR-PaC clinical study, we have the potential to revolutionize the treatment
of pancreatic cancer, shifting patients&rsquo; focus from coping with the treatment and its side-effects, to enjoying more time with
their family and loved ones.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Mr.
Bagai continued, &ldquo;The most significant milestone to date for our therapy platform is expected during the fourth quarter of this
year: the first prospective interim analysis for this pivotal Phase 3 study. This data will provide us with important insight into the
potential for RenovoTAMP at a juncture in the trial equivalent to a robust Phase 2 oncology study, with the rigor of having it randomized.
We have also submitted a protocol for a Phase 2/3 clinical trial in extrahepatic (or outside the liver) cholangiocarcinoma to
FDA &ndash; advancing our therapy platform to other indications. We plan to commence the study and enroll the first patient during the
fourth quarter of 2022, assuming the protocol is acceptable to FDA.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;<FONT STYLE="background-color: white">To
support our growth and infrastructure, in July, we </FONT>added James Ahlers, an accomplished life sciences finance leader, as Chief
Financial Officer, and expanded our finance team with the addition of Ron Kocak, <FONT STYLE="background-color: white">a seasoned financial
reporting and accounting professional,</FONT> as Vice President &amp; Controller,&rdquo; said Mr. Bagai<FONT STYLE="background-color: white">.
&ldquo;With the addition of James and Ron, we continue to build the</FONT> foundation to support the evolution of our clinical pipeline.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Financial
Highlights for the Quarter Ended June 30, 2022</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse">

    of June 30, 2022, the Company had cash and cash equivalents and short-term marketable securities of $10.8 million.</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Research
    and development expenses were $1.4 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2022, compared to $0.5 million for the quarter ended June
    30, 2021. The $0.9 million increase was primarily due to a $0.5 million increase in preclinical research and development and regulatory
    expenses, and a $0.2 million increase in clinical consulting to support the ongoing Phase 3 trial.</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>

    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">General
    and administrative expenses were $1.2 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2022, compared to $0.3 million for the quarter ended
    June 30, 2021. This $0.9 million increase was primarily due to a $0.4 million increase in professional and consulting services related
    to post-IPO support, and a $0.2 million increase for higher personnel related costs.</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>

  <TR STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>About
the Phase 3 TIGeR-PaC Clinical Trial</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">TIGeR-PaC
is a randomized multi-center Phase 3 study using RenovoRx&rsquo;s innovative therapy platform, RenovoTAMP</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><SUP>TM
</SUP><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">(RenovoRx Trans-Arterial Micro-Perfusion). The study is evaluating the Company&rsquo;s first
product candidate, RenovoGem</FONT><SUP>TM</SUP><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">, to treat locally advanced pancreatic cancer (LAPC)
through the intra-arterial delivery of gemcitabine (FDA-approved chemotherapy). The study has a primary endpoint of overall survival
and several secondary endpoints, including quality of life.</FONT></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">TIGeR-PaC
is currently enrolling unresectable LAPC patients at several sites across the US. To learn more about the study and the participating
clinical trial sites, visit </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><U>https://renovorx.com/clinical-trial/</U><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">.</FONT></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>About
RenovoRx, Inc.</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">RenovoRx
is a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on fighting cancer through the localized treatment of difficult to treat tumors
via its proprietary RenovoRx Trans-Arterial Micro-Perfusion (RenovoTAMP<SUP>TM</SUP>) therapy platform. RenovoTAMP utilizes approved
chemotherapeutics with validated mechanisms of action and well-established safety and side effect profiles, with the goal of increasing
their efficacy, improving their safety, and widening their therapeutic window. RenovoRx&rsquo;s lead product candidate, RenovoGem<SUP>TM</SUP>,
is a combination of gemcitabine and our patented delivery system, RenovoCath<SUP>&reg;</SUP>, and is regulated by the FDA as a novel
oncology drug product to treat unresectable locally advanced pancreatic cancer (LAPC). RenovoGem is currently being studied in the Phase
3 TIGeR-PaC trial for the treatment of LAPC.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">RenovoRx&rsquo;s
patent portfolio for its therapy platform and product candidates includes seven U.S. patents, one European patent and several additional
patents pending in the US, EU and Asia. RenovoRx has been granted Orphan Drug Designation for intra-arterial delivery of gemcitabine
for the treatment of both pancreatic cancer and bile duct cancer.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">RenovoRx
won the Drug Delivery Technology category of the Fierce Innovation Awards &ndash; Life Sciences Edition 2020 for its RenovoTAMP technology.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Learn
more by visiting the RenovoRx <U>website</U> or following us on <U>Facebook</U>, <U>LinkedIn</U> and <U>Twitter</U>.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
